<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missing.html>missing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:please.html>Please</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:add.html>add</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discuss.html>discuss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></i>, alteration <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tinde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tind</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tind</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tindaz</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tinnitus.html>tinnitus</a> (87331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tinnītus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> jingling, ringing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tinnitus.html>tinnitus</a></strong> (<i>countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tinnituses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> perception <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noise.html>noise</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:such.html>such</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> ringing <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> beating <a href = vnd.unilang:sound.html>sound</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:no.html>no</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:external.html>external</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:source.html>source</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***tochtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tochtig.html>tochtig</a> (50515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tuchtich</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tochtig.html>tochtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tochtig.html>tochtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">tochtigst</b>)
</p>
